## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the population growth rate (dP/dt) as a function of time (t) and current population size (P). This is a classic population dynamics problem where growth rate depends on population size through density-dependent feedback mechanisms, and possibly on time through environmental forcing.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Exponential (Malthusian) growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Density-independent growth, unlimited resources'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decreasing logarithmically with population size'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Allee effect growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Population with critical minimum threshold for positive growth'}
- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Growth as balance between anabolism and catabolism with allometric scaling'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Flexible asymmetric sigmoidal growth'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent Malthusian rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Exponential growth with time-varying growth rate'}
- {'name': 'Seasonal/oscillatory modulated growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t))', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth with periodic environmental forcing'}
- {'name': 'Power-law growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Allometric or fractal-like population growth dynamics'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2', 'scenario': 'Simple polynomial density-dependent growth'}
- {'name': 'Beverton-Holt continuous analog', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Growth with saturating reproduction minus linear mortality'}
- {'name': 'Declining growth with time', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Resource depletion causing growth rate to decline over time'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback â†’ multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) reducing growth at high P
- Allee effect (positive density dependence at low P) â†’ factor (P - c) creating a growth minimum threshold
- Logarithmic saturation in growth â†’ log(c/P) term as in Gompertz models
- Time-varying carrying capacity or growth rate â†’ multiplicative time-dependent modulation such as (1 + c*sin(c*t)) or exp(c*t)
- Allometric scaling in metabolism â†’ fractional power P**c1 with c1 â‰  1 reflecting body-size or resource scaling
- Competition or crowding effects â†’ P**2 or higher-order polynomial terms in P representing pairwise interactions
- Balance of production and loss â†’ difference of two power-law terms c0*P**a - c1*P**b representing anabolism vs catabolism
- Saturating per-capita growth â†’ rational form c0*P/(c1+P) where per-capita rate declines hyperbolically
